The Suppression of Bandits in Eastern Fujian Has Entered its Final Stage 23

The Pacification of the Fu'an to Shouning Region

Li Mo'an Convenes a Pacification Conference

[Fuzhou] Military intelligence indicates that the suppression of bandits in eastern Fujian has entered its final stage. The remaining bandits in the Fu'an to Shouning region have been pacified. Currently, efforts are focused on reconstruction, including the construction of碉堡 (fortified structures) and the pursuit of scattered bandits. The Fourth District Command reported on the 17th, based on a telegram from Regiment Commander Chen Peiyu, that Feng Pintai's bandit gang had fled to Dafu, under the jurisdiction of Shouning County, and coordinated with Zhang Hejin's gang, which had fled to Xiyang, under the jurisdiction of Fu'an County. After being defeated in Xiyang and scattered, they were pursued. The defense area is gradually being pacified. Locals are now being supervised to build碉堡 (fortified structures) at strategic points. The Third Battalion has been ordered to continue to suppress the bandits. Upon receiving the report, the provincial authorities have ordered all armies to coordinate and encircle the scattered bandits to eradicate them completely. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

[Fuzhou] Feng Pintai's bandit gang fled in defeat to Xiaoyang, Fu'an. The provincial authorities have ordered all armies in eastern Fujian to encircle and suppress them to eradicate them completely. Huang Ligui's bandits, who have been harassing the border of Chong'an, have been pursued and suppressed by Zhou Zhiqun's division, advancing through Xingqiao, Shangxia Mei. The main force of the bandits has been largely annihilated, and the remaining bandits will not be difficult to eliminate. (Special dispatch, 17th)

[Fuzhou] Chen Peiyu telegraphed that the bandits in Shouning County have been largely eliminated after a fierce suppression by our army. However, there are still six scattered bandit gangs in Qinglong, Yintan, and other places, each with fewer than a hundred members. They are currently being pursued and suppressed. (Special dispatch, 18th)

[Fuzhou] Li Mo'an, the commander of the Second Pacification Zone stationed in Longyan, has scheduled a pacification conference around the 25th, inviting the division and brigade commanders under his jurisdiction, as well as the magistrates of Longyan, Yongding, Liancheng, Tingzhou, and six other counties, to Longyan. He has already issued orders to collect and submit proposals. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

[Xiamen] The Pacification Headquarters received a telegram from Zhang Wanji of the Independent 45th Brigade, reporting that on the 14th, they recovered the lairs of the local communists in Chong'an, including Da'an, Chongyong, and Dahunqing, successively, killing over 700 bandits and capturing over 50. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Hubei Provincial Government to Establish Xiangyang Group Farms 25

[Hankou] The provincial government has decided to establish Xiangyang Group Farms, based on the principle of "land to the tiller." Those who reclaim land must cultivate it themselves absolutely, eliminating the boundaries between landowners, self-cultivating farmers, tenant farmers, and hired laborers. The county has over 300,000 acres of wasteland. The original reclamation agencies have been abolished. If Xiangyang is successful on the 16th, it will be implemented in Jingshan and Jingmen as well. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Remarks by the American Ambassador to Reporters in Nanjing 26

The United States is Studying Ways to Resolve the Silver Problem

The Revised Sino-American Commercial Treaty Has Not Yet Received Instructions

[Nanjing] American Ambassador Johnson, who took leave to return to the United States last June, arrived in Nanjing on the evening of the 17th. On the 18th, Mr. Johnson stated that he was in the United States for about three months, spending the most time in Washington. He also visited New York and various rural areas. Due to the economic recession in recent years, the country has been spending huge sums of money annually for relief. This time, he visited various villages, from the west to the east, and each village had signs of "work-for-relief" to repair various tree beams and roads. The unemployment problem is gradually being solved. Both in cities and villages, there is a gradual sense of prosperity compared to before. In general, the economy of our country is gradually showing signs of recovery. It is expected that the atmosphere of the past recession will be swept away this autumn. A reporter inquired about the revision of the Sino-American Commercial Treaty. The Ambassador had previously indicated when he returned to the United States that he would proceed after seeking instructions. What is the current situation? Johnson replied that there has been no progress in revising the Sino-American Commercial Treaty of 1903. He has not received any instructions to proceed with this matter, so it is difficult to answer at this time. When asked about the issue of the Embassy moving south, he said that the American Embassy in Nanjing has an office, and Consul General Peck is his representative. He also comes to Nanjing often, which can be considered as the Embassy being in Nanjing. As for the Embassy in Beijing, there is currently no intention to move it. Finally, someone inquired about the opinion of the Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota on Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. Johnson replied that he only saw it in the newspaper and did not know the actual situation. He had not heard about the government's opinion on this issue when he was in the United States. He dared not express any opinions on this issue in his official capacity and could not express any opinions. (Special dispatch, 18th)

[Nanjing] American Ambassador Johnson arrived in Nanjing on the evening of the 17th. On the morning of the 18th, at 11 o'clock, he met with reporters at the American Consulate General and spoke freely about the American economic situation and the silver issue. According to him, the American economy has been greatly affected by the global economic recession in the past three years and has been very sluggish. Most people are unemployed, and all construction cannot be completed. Recently, the American government has been trying its best to revitalize the national economy and is using the method of "work-for-relief" to carry out various constructions. Regarding the silver issue, the American government and public are currently studying a proper solution. When he passed through New York, economic figures were holding meetings to discuss this issue. The American government is now solving domestic problems, which inevitably affects other parts of the world, but the American government does not want to benefit itself and affect other countries. However, there is a solution for the agricultural industry, namely, currency inflation, to raise prices, and the government will try to help without affecting the interests of other countries. A reporter asked whether the United States had recently changed its silver purchasing policy. He replied that the American government has various difficulties in this regard because it must take into account the domestic situation, but it cannot ignore the foreign environment. A reporter asked whether the implementation of the silver policy was due to the silver group and the representatives of various states considering the interests of the silver-producing states. He said that although the representatives of the silver-producing states are considering their interests, the representatives of the agricultural states in the western United States are also standing in the same position because they want to raise prices and obtain relief. Therefore, the American government must take into account the political power of both sides. Finally, the reporter said that the American silver policy has greatly affected China's economy, and it is hoped that the United States will find a solution to this matter as soon as possible. Ambassador Johnson replied that Roosevelt and his advisors are indeed trying their best to carefully consider a proper solution to avoid affecting the Far East, but they have not yet found a better way. However, this was the situation two months ago when he passed through Washington. He did not know what the recent situation was. He then spoke about the revision of the Sino-American Commercial Treaty. Johnson said that he had not yet received instructions from the government. The American Embassy also has no intention of moving to Nanjing recently because the Consulate General in Nanjing is the Embassy's office in Nanjing. The upgrading of the Sino-American diplomatic missions has not been discussed in Washington. Finally, Johnson said regarding the recent situation in the Far East that the United States sincerely hopes that all countries can be friendly with each other. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

[Nanjing] After arriving in Nanjing, American Ambassador Johnson sent a letter from the American Consulate General in Nanjing to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 18th to request a meeting with the Vice Minister. It is reported that Xu Mo has scheduled a meeting for 10 a.m. on the 20th. The date for the meeting with Minister Wang has not yet been determined. Johnson will stay in Nanjing for ten days before returning to Beijing. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Ministry of Interior Explains Doubts about Copyright Protection 46

Commentary

First Anniversary of the New Life Movement 52

— Year

It has been a year since Generalissimo Chiang delivered a speech at the expanded memorial week in Nanchang on this day last year, advocating the New Life Movement. This New Life Movement, which aims to revitalize the nation and is based on raising the knowledge and morality of the people, has swept the country for a year. The extent of its growth and development is what the people of the country should pay attention to today.

In order to enable the people of the country to understand the progress of the New Life Movement over the past year, this newspaper's yearbook has specially invited Mr. Zhang Xiaotong, who is very knowledgeable in this field, to make a detailed record. The main points are excerpted as follows: (1) Since its inception in Nanchang, it has been followed by 21 provinces and regions under the leadership of Generalissimo Chiang, including the capital Nanjing, Shanghai, Beijing, and major cities, as well as Jiangsu, Hebei, Hubei, Fujian, Anhui, Henan, Zhejiang, Hunan, Shandong, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Chahar, Suiyuan, Ningxia, Qinghai, Sichuan, Guizhou, Yunnan, and Kangding. Of the 28 provinces and regions in the country, the four northeastern provinces are in the midst of being occupied, and Xinjiang is isolated. Therefore, apart from Guangdong and Guangxi, the movement has achieved widespread success. (2) Starting in July last year, the National New Life Movement was changed from being promoted by the Promotion Association to being guided by the General Association. Not only are the steps unified, but the work has also progressed from propaganda to practical action. (3) The initial stage of the New Life Movement requires achieving six items: neatness, cleanliness, simplicity, frugality, speed, and certainty. By the end of 1934, the initial stage of "orderliness" and "cleanliness" had come to an end and entered a further stage of militarizing, industrializing, and artisticizing life.

In summary, the achievements of the New Life Movement over the past year are clearly visible. Let's further examine its content. In the "Outline of the New Life Movement," there is an explanation of this:

The New Life Movement is to promote "a disciplined life of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame." The virtues of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame are practiced in daily life - in the four things of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame are the center of rules for developing people's virtue to accomplish people's work, for treating people, handling affairs, maintaining oneself, and dealing with things.

When the people of the country read these few words, it is not difficult to get a concrete idea of ​​the content of the new life. In other words, this is actually a movement to rationalize life. If the lives of the 470 million people in the country can gradually tend to be rationalized, then the corrupt will be honest, the weak will be strong, the people's virtue will be shown daily, and the people's strength will be increased daily. The goal of revitalizing the nation may be achieved. However, this requires the people of the country to thoroughly realize the unreasonable accumulated life. Every citizen starts from themselves, washing away the filth and dirt. The focus of the effort is entirely on the word "do."

Generalissimo Chiang said in his speech on this day last year: "...The purpose of the New Life Movement is to thoroughly militarize the lives of all the people in the country... I hope that everyone will make a decision to die yesterday and be born today, and thoroughly reform all the barbaric lives of the past that were not suitable for modernization. Everything new life, new movement, new career, all start from today..." Rerecord this statement to encourage the people of the country and to replace the congratulatory message on the anniversary.

The Japanese-Puppet Regime's New Regulations on Banning Chinese Laborers from Entering 関 Are Implemented Tomorrow 53

[Dalian] The puppet organization is scheduled to implement the "Regulations on the Control of Foreign Laborers" on the 20th of this month. The Japanese authorities in the Kwantung Leased Territory are also scheduled to implement the "Regulations on Foreign Laborers" on the same day. The purpose is to prevent workers from 関内 (China proper, south of the Great Wall) from seeking work in the Northeast. According to Japanese investigations, the number of North China workers who went to 関外 (the Northeast, north of the Great Wall) in the spring and returned to their hometowns in the autumn each year peaked at 1.13 million in 1928. After the September 18th Incident, it has seen a sharp decrease, but there were still more than 570,000 people last year. The amount of money that workers bring back or remit to 関内 each year averages more than 20 million yuan. At the same time, it has caused the inflow of puppet currency into 関内, and Japan has also suffered great losses as a result. Therefore, regulations have been promulgated to only allow workers with specialized skills to enter 関, and it is planned to set up control agencies in Dalian, Yingkou, Andong, Shanhaiguan, Gubeikou, and Xifengkou. (Hualian Telegram, 18th)

A Large Gold Mine Discovered in the Upper Reaches of the Hunchun River 54

The Estimated Reserves are Worth 200 Million Yuan

Japanese Companies Forcibly Seize the Operating Rights of Chinese People

[Changchun] According to news from the Manchurian Gold Mining Company, the company discovered a high-quality gold mine in the upper reaches of the Hunchun River in eastern Jilin. The mine was originally operated by Chinese people on a small scale. After the company tested the mine, it believed that the amount of gold buried was as high as 200 million yuan. Therefore, it forcibly took over with a small amount of capital and decided to transport machinery and start gold mining recently. (Hualian Telegram, 18th)

Accident at Japanese Military Factory 55

More Than Ten Naval Aircraft Burned Down

Losses Reach More Than One Million Yuan

According to Hualian President Nagasaki Tsu, at 8:40 p.m. on the 11th, an accident occurred at the Watanabe Iron Works outside Fukuoka City. The fire was not extinguished until 10:30 p.m. More than ten naval aircraft built by the factory were all destroyed. The total of other losses amounted to more than one million yuan. The factory is an important military factory. The navy suffered a huge blow this time. After the accident, the army was dispatched to strictly guard against the leakage of military secrets. The cause of the fire seems to be arson.

War is Difficult to Avoid in the Italian Military Expedition to East Africa 57

Messina Has Become a Large Military Camp

Troops Depart Singing War Songs

The African war seems difficult to avoid. Today, three battalions of the fascist militia and the 3rd Regiment of the Guerro di Lorena Division, totaling 3,000 men, embarked on the transport ship Bianco Mano Boro bound for North Africa. Messina has now become a large military camp. Young people from all over arrive by train every day. They are eager to go to Africa to protect Italian interests. It is not yet known how many troops the Italian authorities will send, but if the number sent is still considered small, there are many troops in Messina. They can depart as soon as they receive orders. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

Two thousand Italian soldiers from Naples embarked on the Italian ship Ganges today, bound for Italian Somaliland in Africa. They are expected to arrive at their destination on February 24. All schools have been closed so that students can see the soldiers marching through the city. The streets were crowded with onlookers. General Ferrucci, the deputy commander of the Italian National Militia, inspected the troops before their departure. When the troops passed in front of him, they all raised their hands in salute. As the Ganges departed, all the churches rang their bells and all the ships in the port sounded their horns to show their farewells. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

The Italian transport ship Ganges departed from the port of Naples at noon today, carrying two battalions of the Fascist Party army, bound for Massawa in Italian Eritrea, Africa. Many other officers also departed on the ship. At the time of departure, all ships in the port hung flags to celebrate, and the whistles sounded in unison. The masses on the scene cheered enthusiastically, and colorful banners were hung everywhere in the city, with posters in the three colors of the national flag pasted on the walls. Also, because the schools were closed, there were many young children mixed in the crowd. The two battalions of the Party army, before boarding the ship, were stationed at the Clarini Barracks. This barracks is a red building, large in scale, originally built by the French Baben Wangbao and used as a warehouse. The Party army paraded in formation, led by the military band of the 133rd Regiment, playing the Neapolitan song "Marina Tripoli" made during the 1912 war between Italy and the Libyan region of Africa. The soldiers of the Party army rose and danced when they heard the horn, inserting flowers on their guns and small pieces of paper on their helmets. The Ganges also carried 200 tons of equipment and many mules and horses, and is expected to arrive in Massawa next Sunday. (Havas Dispatch, 18th)

Beyond the Scope of Self-Defense 58

Since the Fascist Party's Supreme Council decided to send three battalions of troops to Northeast Africa, it is believed here that there will be large-scale military operations in the future. The reason why Mussolini sent volunteers to Africa is to make his regular army ready for contingencies in Central Europe. Martin believes that the steps taken by Italy so far have exceeded the scope of self-defense, and the purpose may not only be to obtain reparations, but may have more ambitious goals. (National Telegram, 18th)

Military Supplies Prepared for Any Eventuality 59

[Rome] After holding meetings for several days, the Supreme Council of the Fascist Party issued a communique, stating that the government has taken all necessary measures to maintain and increase the army's strength. The intention of this communique is to point out that Italy's military manufacturing has already increased its quantity, prepared for any eventuality. It is generally believed that the current situation in Europe has not yet been fully clarified. After a large number of military supplies are transported to East Africa, the national defense of Europe will be a concern. Now, after this statement, this concern can be dispelled. It is generally estimated that Italy can immediately dispatch 70,000 troops to Africa, and 30,000 more can be trained later. (Havas Dispatch, 17th)

Compulsory Military Training for Men 60

[Rome] The Fascist Grand Council has resolved that Italian men between the ages of six and fifty-five should undergo military training. It is said that this is a major step taken by Mussolini to unite and instill Fascist ideology into the people. A large proportion of Italians will be affected, as well as any civilians with some military value. According to the laws, Italian men of a certain age are already required to receive military training, but this new resolution is as thorough as the Soviet Union's compulsory study of communism. Some observers say that the Italian-Ethiopian war may be a factor in this move. (18th National Telegram)

Italian Troops Increase Defense of Austria 61

[Paris] It is quite believable that Germany is currently making worrying preparations in the Tyrol province on the Austrian border. The Vienna correspondent of the Daily Telegraph reports that three divisions of troops from Bavaria, Germany, have begun to mobilize. Italy has also mobilized two armies on the Italian-Austrian border, paying particular attention to the Brenner Pass. It is said that Mussolini issued this sudden mobilization order because he feared that the National Socialist Party would take the opportunity to start an uprising in Austria while Italian troops were being sent to North Africa. (18th Havas Telegram)

[Rome] The Vienna correspondent of the Daily Telegraph has sent news stating that Italy has mobilized two armies on the Italian-Austrian border, especially near the Brenner Pass. This has been reported in another telegram. Semi-official sources here deny this news, but tacitly acknowledge that necessary measures have been taken to strengthen border defenses. Although Rome has not heard of any alarms outside the border, border defense cannot be neglected because Italian troops have begun to deploy to Africa. As for the mobilization measures taken due to the Italian-Ethiopian conflict, soldiers of the 1911 class are being successively called up by name. In addition, mobilization work technically involves soldiers of other classes, and preparations are being made for their call-up. However, at present, except for soldiers of the 1911 class, volunteers, and technicians, no other call-ups have been implemented. (18th Havas Telegram)

Russian Pravda Reports the Truth of the Anti-Japanese Resistance 65

[Moscow] Reporting on the battles of the anti-Japanese volunteer army in Manchuria, Pravda says, "Special attention must be paid to these wars. As a rule, the wave of rebellion inevitably decreases every winter because the weather in Manchuria is too cold, and the rebels lack food and clothing and cannot advance quickly. However, 1934 was the most difficult year for the working masses in Manchuria. Millions of hungry and exhausted farmers flowed from the countryside to the cities, and thousands of them joined the rebel ranks. They disregarded the severe cold and advanced towards Shenyang, Jinzhou, and Jilin. This was completely unexpected by the Japanese military authorities. A month ago, Japanese newspapers claimed that the rebels in Manchuria had been completely eliminated." Therefore, Pravda concludes, "This report is premature." (17th TASS Telegram) [Shenyang] It is reported that at 10 AM this morning, 50 members of the volunteer army attacked Japanese police at Xiaohedao, eight miles west of Shenyang, killing one Japanese police officer. (18th China United News Agency Telegram)

Japan Forms Committee to Discuss Countermeasures to Naval Conference 67

[Tokyo] The Asahi Shimbun reports that Naval Minister Osumi has instructed the Naval Policy Committee to re-examine the possibility of reconciling Japan's claims with those of Britain and the United States in March. The committee will invite Yamamoto, who participated in the London Naval Talks, to attend a joint discussion. The considerations are: (1) What plan should Japan adopt if it builds a navy to a limit of 1.1 million tons? (2) Study the reasons why Britain and the United States oppose Japan's complete abolition of naval offensive weapons. (3) Compare the opinions of Britain, the United States, and Japan on qualitative and quantitative disarmament. (4) Review the possibility of extending or abolishing the agreement on Pacific defense projects. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Japanese Consideration

Abolishing Consular Jurisdiction in Manchuria 69

[Tokyo] According to responsible sources, a committee recently formed by Shigemitsu Kure and officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of the Army, the Ministry of Justice, and others is studying how Japan should abolish its consular jurisdiction in Manchuria. It will choose between a unilateral declaration and a special agreement with "Manchukuo." (18th Reuters Telegram)

China United News Agency Tokyo Dispatch: The Japanese government organized a committee on February 13th to investigate the abolition of extraterritoriality in puppet Manchukuo. The chairman is Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Shigemitsu. It is heard that the outline of the withdrawal plan is as follows: (1) Japan will abolish civil and criminal jurisdiction after puppet Manchukuo implements major laws and modern court and prison systems. (2) The abolition of jurisdiction will exclude the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Zone. (3) However, before puppet Manchukuo fully possesses a judicial system, Japanese defendants must be tried by Japanese judges. (4) After Japan abolishes jurisdiction, it must recognize that Japanese people have the right to do business and reside throughout puppet Manchukuo, and enjoy the right to own real estate and all related rights. (5) When Japan completely abolishes extraterritoriality, it will recognize puppet Manchukuo's administrative rights in the South Manchuria Railway Zone, but for a certain period, puppet Manchukuo must compensate Japanese residents in the affiliated territories for their losses.

Regaining Fifteen Years of Financial Power: Saar Customs Under German Jurisdiction, Swastika Flags Fly, Torch Parade, Germans Cheer to Celebrate 77

Full Text of Franco-German Agreement Published

The Saarbrücken-Saar area, which has been under the jurisdiction of French customs, has been transferred to German customs jurisdiction from today. French customs personnel completely withdrew from the border between the Saar area and Germany at midnight yesterday. At the same time, 500 German customs personnel set up customs and levied taxes on the border between France and the Saar area. The exchange was peaceful and without incident. (18th Havas Telegram)

The customs at the border between Saarbrücken-Saar and Germany, which have been in place for fifteen years, have finally come to an end. At the same time, after the German customs organization at the border between the Saar and France was announced, it was declared established at midnight yesterday. Five hundred German customs officers also took up their respective positions. Although the ceremony was held at midnight, there were many people participating. The German national flag flew over the top of the customs house amidst the cheers of the crowd. There was also a grand torch parade that night to commemorate the occasion. (18th National Telegram)

Signing of the Agreement 78

In Naples, Italy, the Franco-German agreement on the Saar issue was initialed the night before last and formally signed this morning at the Excelsior Hotel here. Aloisi, Chairman of the Three-Person Committee on the Saar issue, Lopez, and Argentine Ambassador Astengo, representing the Saar Administrative Committee Chairman Knox, sat at one end of the table. French Ambassador to Italy Chambrun and German Ambassador to Italy Hassell sat at the other end. Personnel from the League of Nations Secretariat were also present. Aloisi, the chairman of the Three-Person Committee, addressed the French and German negotiators, as well as various experts and Knox, congratulating them on their success. The first signature was that of German Ambassador to Italy Hassell, at 10:15 AM. The signing was completed successively at 10:35 AM. After the ceremony, the ambassadors and members of the Three-Person Committee boarded the destroyer "Chen Ji Long" to go to Capri for lunch. A total of four agreements, including fourteen annexes, were signed today. The first agreement stipulates that France will transfer its ownership of all mineral resources, railways, and other real estate in the Saar to Germany. The second agreement relates to French private social insurance in the Saar. The third agreement is for transitional measures for social insurance. The fourth agreement is concluded between the Saar Administrative Committee and Germany to stipulate the transfer of Saar administrative power. (18th Havas Telegram)

[Rome] The full text of the agreement on the transfer and merger of the Saar region into Germany's economic issues was published here today. The formal signing of the agreement has also been scheduled by the League of Nations' Three-Person Committee, with the support of Chairman Alci. It will be held in Naples tomorrow. It is heard that the agreement is divided into five sections. The first section describes the transfer of Saar mineral resources and railways to Germany, with a price of 900 million francs. The method of payment, partly in cash and partly in goods, especially coal, has also been specified in detail. In addition, appropriate measures have been planned for the exchange of currencies. The current French banknotes will be exchanged for German currency and recorded in the French bank account as part of the 900 million franc debt. The second section of the agreement involves social insurance matters. The third section describes the issue of the survival and disposal of private insurance businesses in the Saar region. The fourth section concerns the continued mining of coal mines in the Walent district by French private companies, as well as the continued employment of German miners and the application of the management regulations of the French companies. Regarding this matter, if there is a dispute over the interpretation of the treaty text regarding the quantity of coal extracted in the district in the future, it has been stipulated that Aloisi will be appointed as an arbitrator. The fifth section contains the procedures for the transfer of the French administrative organs to the German authorities. (17th National Telegram)

German Sex Espionage Case 81

Beautiful and Flattering Polish Officer

Baroness Falls in Love

Inducing Noble Women to Be Used

Military Secrets Leaked, Social Flower Beheaded

[Berlin] Baroness Berg and Mrs. Nazzena were sentenced to death after being accused of selling Germany's entire mobilization plan to a certain foreign country. If German leader Hitler does not grant leniency, they will be executed today. After the execution, the charges will be announced. It is heard that the means used for espionage are like materials from novels. First, Baroness Berg became acquainted with a Polish officer named Sosnowski, who was addicted to gambling, skilled at riding, and beautiful and flattering. Before long, the baroness fell in love and could not extricate herself, and she willingly ran around to seek out military secrets. Her plan was very poisonous. The baroness made many female friends in social circles, many of whom were daughters of senior military officers and officials of the Army Department. She invited these women every day to indulge in drinking and introduced them to young men. Those with weak wills engaged in illicit behavior, and the baroness secretly took their photos and showed them to them. For the sake of their faces, these women had no choice but to obey her. As for Mrs. Nazzena, she was also an accomplice of Sosnowski. (17th Reuters Telegram)

[Berlin] Two famous German socialites, one being Mrs. Folkerheim, formerly Baroness Berg, who divorced two weeks ago, and the other being Mrs. Nazzena, were found guilty by a military court on Saturday and Sunday of engaging in espionage activities in collusion with Polish officer Baron Sosnowski and sentenced to death. German leader Hitler did not want to grant leniency, so they were beheaded this morning in front of the prison here. Two others, one being Mrs. Gena and the other being the Polish officer, were accomplices and were sentenced to life imprisonment with hard labor. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Russian Newspaper Harshly Criticizes England, Holding it Responsible for European War 82

Permitting Germany's Military Equality on One Hand,

While Tacitly Approving its Freedom in Eastern Europe

The So-Called Air Pact Creates War Opportunities

[Moscow] Izvestia commented on Germany's reply to the Anglo-French proposal, saying, "Germany's reply is even worse than the expectations of the most pessimistic observers of the current situation." The newspaper quoted the Anglo-French press on the German reply, saying, "Germany's attitude and the comments of the English newspapers on its reply are clearly in collusion, and the latter can indeed reflect the opinions of the British government authorities. The British authorities are willing to allow Germany military equality (meaning arming it) while allowing it freedom of action in Eastern Europe. In other words, the British authorities are willing to encourage Hitler's aggressive ambitions for German fascism, which he clearly stipulated in his book 'Mein Kampf.' This attitude of the UK is a powerful blow to France, as we all know that 'peace is indivisible.'"

"If Germany is allowed freedom of action in Eastern Europe today, Germany will allow itself freedom of action in Western Europe tomorrow. In this way, the Little Entente countries will have no security. This means that France's position on the European continent will be greatly weakened. At the same time, if Germany attacks Czechoslovakia and France will aid Czechoslovakia because of the alliance treaty, then according to the original intention of the Air Pact, which deviated from the London Agreement, Britain will attack France. Therefore, the British authorities' attack on the Eastern European Pact is also an attack on France. The German reply has another purpose, which is to eliminate France's credibility with its allies and friends. When Berlin drafted the reply, it claimed that the gist of its reply was in line with British hopes and that it was willing to cooperate with Britain to get France out of its current position and weaken it. If the spirit of the London proposal is as expected in the German reply, then its impact on peace will be extremely serious and great. The air pact between Germany, France, and England cannot prevent war; on the contrary, it creates war crises and intensifies them several times. This is because it grants freedom of action to German imperialists. The British authorities are consolidating the position of the enemies of peace under the guise of maintaining peace. Therefore, the British authorities should bear full responsibility for maintaining European peace," (TASS dispatch, 17th).

[London] Since the publication of Germany's reply to the Anglo-French suggestions, British newspapers seemed to hope that discussions between the UK and Germany could be held. However, they also believed that the situation created by the German reply was quite chaotic. If the UK was too eager, it would be rash. The Daily Telegraph reported, "If Foreign Secretary Simon goes to Berlin, Germany's prestige will inevitably increase. But at the present stage, for the sake of practical results, it seems better for Germany to send someone to Britain." The Daily Mail reported, "If talks can be held between the UK and Germany, they would be as appropriate a measure as talks between the UK and France. However, at the current stage, whether UK-German talks would be beneficial is questionable. If we consider it carefully, we think it is better to let things take their natural course for the time being and consider it again after Berlin has replied anew." The Morning Post said, "Under the current circumstances, it would be a waste of time for Foreign Secretary Simon to go to Berlin or for German Foreign Minister Neurath to come here." The newspaper also criticized the Soviet Union in a pessimistic tone, saying that the country was only seeking its own interests, hindering France's freedom of action, and even sowing discord among Western European countries, which was inappropriate. The newspaper also launched a fierce attack on Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov (Havas dispatch, 18th).

American Prisoners Escape 83

Shoot and Kill a Jailer

Escape in Separate Cars

Only Three of Twenty-One Are Recaptured

Twenty-one prisoners from the Granite Youth Prison shot and killed a jailer at the Oklahoma Reformatory today. Warden Ms. Walter immediately ordered a search. Several hours later, three escapees were arrested. It has been gradually becoming more popular in the United States for women to manage prisons, which is being hotly debated in the field of criminal law. This prison escape will add information to the history of women managing prisons. It is also recalled that the king of assassins, Dillinger, killed and injured many after escaping from the Crown Point prison before finally being shot in Chicago. At that time, the warden of Crown Point prison was Ms. Holley. Officials were shocked today after hearing about the prison escape. The escapees had obviously made careful arrangements beforehand. The circumstances of the incident are recorded below: Initially, the prisoners forced the jailer to not report the escape. After shooting him, they broke down the walls in groups of two or three, got into three cars, and drove away quickly. Ms. Walter immediately ordered a search and sent armed jailers in cars to chase down the escapees. All the police in the state of Oklahoma were ordered to guard the main roads. Ms. Walter said that she hoped to capture the escapees within a few hours (National Telegram, 17th).

Disaster Victims in Eastern and Southern Hubei Die One After Another 104

Many Starved Disaster Victims in Huangmei Resemble a Ghost Land

Relief Association's Inspection and Distribution Office Asks for More Funds for Relief

Hankou Correspondence: The drought in Hubei Province last year was extremely severe. The counties in eastern and southern Hubei had no harvest, and the number of disaster victims who could not survive without relief reached four to five million. Although the government authorities and charitable organizations made efforts to provide relief, the funds were too few and the people were too many, making it difficult to achieve universal coverage. In addition to Yangxin County, where 1,800 people died of starvation, deaths also occurred daily in Huangmei, Huang'an, Macheng, Lishan, Wuchang, Hanyang, Tongshan, Tongcheng, Chongyang, Puji, Xianning, Daye, Huanggang, Echeng, Qichun, Guangji, Luotian, Yingshan, Huangpi, Xiaogan, and other counties. Now that the spring famine is coming to an end, everything has been exhausted, and even more people are dying. The situation in the disaster areas is difficult to describe in full detail based only on telegram reports. The reporter recently went to eastern Hubei for business and passed through Huangmei, the county most severely affected by the disaster. The reporter entered the countryside to investigate and saw that the disaster victims were eating things like white clay, tree bark, and grass roots. They did not know the taste of salt and rice. Their clothes were full of patches, and they slept on grass. The walls of their homes were full of holes, not sheltering them from the wind and rain. Some even lived in cattle pens, pig sheds, or broken boats. Livestock had long been slaughtered, and chickens were rarely seen, resembling a ghost land. The reporter also saw a woman named Shi carrying her young son to the market, weeping uncontrollably. Old and weak disaster victims were dying every day, five or six people to more than ten people, and they were hastily buried and left on the roads. The tragic situation made it unbearable to hear or see. If Huangmei is like this, other places can also be inferred.

The Shanghai Drought Relief Association for Various Provinces has established an inspection and distribution office in Hubei. The 150,000 yuan allocated was only distributed to eight counties and districts, including Yangxin, which was not enough. Fourteen counties, including Tongshan, are still waiting. The office urgently telegraphed the Shanghai Association yesterday, requesting additional funds for relief. The telegram stated that the 150,000 yuan allocated to Hubei Province had been fully distributed to eight counties and districts, including Yangxin, Huangmei, Huang'an, Macheng, Lishan, Wuchang, Hanyang, and the Dapan Special District, in accordance with the principle of "saving the dying, not the poor" and providing relief to the elderly, weak, disabled, and others over 50 years old and under 15 years old who could not survive without relief. Even with the distribution to eight counties, it was still not enough. The disaster in Hubei Province is severe, and the disaster area is vast. It is impossible to help only the disaster victims in eight counties. According to recent investigations, the disaster situation in Tongshan, Tongcheng, Chongyang, Puji, Xianning, and Dazhi in southern Hubei, as well as Huanggang, Echeng, Qichun, Guangji, Luotian, Yingshan, Huangpi, and Xiaogan in eastern Hubei, is no less severe than that in Yangxin and Huangma. After suffering from banditry, these counties suffered a drought, and 80-90% of the people were displaced and had no smoke rising from their chimneys. In this freezing weather, there is no bark to peel from the trees and no grass to dig from the ground. The cries of hunger and cold can be heard everywhere, and the white bones on the roadside are all innocent, starving ghosts. It is not just a matter of abandoning wives and selling children and eating soil. Therefore, we have no choice but to ask the association to approve the allocation of more funds to help them survive and expand relief (17th).

Taiwan's Trade Increases Sharply 105

Nearly 20 Million More Than the Same Period Last Year

Japanese Tea Production Also Increases Dramatically

Xiamen Correspondence: According to a survey by the Financial Bureau of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, the total amount of Taiwan's foreign trade in January of this year was 58,923,028 yuan, an increase of 19,450,785 yuan compared to the 39,472,243 yuan in January of last year. Among them, foreign trade accounted for 5,659,558 yuan, an increase of 6,9063 yuan compared to January of last year. In terms of imports and exports, exports were 2,424,359 yuan, an increase of 986,870 yuan compared to the same period last year, and imports were 3,235,219 yuan, a decrease of 917,807 yuan compared to the same period last year. The increase in exports in January was due to the rise in silver prices and the export of various intermediary trade products, while imports decreased sharply. The total amount of domestic trade (that is, Taiwan's trade with Japan) in January was 53,263,470 yuan, an increase of 19,381,712 yuan compared to the 33,882,748 yuan in January of last year. This was mainly due to the increase in the export (i.e., export to Japan) of major products such as rice and sugar, as well as the increase in the import of cotton fabrics, fertilizers, and food from the mainland (Japan).

In recent years, the production of black tea in Shizuoka and Taiwan has increased dramatically. In 1933, Shizuoka's black tea production was only 128,662 catties, while Taiwan's was only 1,372,797 catties. In 1934, Shizuoka's production jumped to 2,193,907 catties, an increase of 17 times. Taiwan also increased to 5,494,220 catties, an increase of 5 times. Although the price in 1933 was higher than in 1934, the rapid and significant increase in quantity shows the dramatic expansion of Japanese tea (February 13th).

The Jingwu Railway is Scheduled to Open to Traffic Next Month 106

Zhang Jingjiang Inspects the Jingwu and Wusun Projects

Wuhu Correspondence: The Jiangnan Railway Company is building the Jingzhao Railway, which starts from the capital in the north and connects to Fujian and Guangdong in the south, running north-south for more than a thousand miles. The section from Wuhu to Sunjiabu in Jiangsu and Anhui has already been opened to traffic. After the contract for cargo transport was signed with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to handle combined shipping between Wuhu and Shanghai, it was implemented the day before yesterday. Passengers are also participating in the four-way combined transport with the Jingwu Highway and the Jinghu Railway Bureau. It is extremely convenient for travelers from Xuancheng and Sunjiabu to travel to Beijing, Shanghai, and other places. The progress of the Jingwu section of the project has also been very rapid. The Dangtu River Bridge, a major project, was also completed the other day. Material vehicles have passed over the bridge and reached the north bank, laying tracks towards Beijing. After the sleepers are laid, vehicles between Beijing and Wuhu can simultaneously run on the bridge. The entire section of road construction is expected to be completed by March of this year. Zhang Jingjiang, the general manager of the company, along with Section Chief Qin of the Central Construction Committee and managers Pang Zan成 and others, departed from Beijing on the morning of the 12th in two cars to inspect the line. They arrived in Dangtu at 7:00 PM and carefully surveyed the bridge. They then transferred to a special car sent by the company to greet them in Wuhu, summoned officials from the general affairs, engineering, and transportation departments to consult on the project's progress. It was pointed out that this road is of great importance to the development of production in the southern provinces. In this time of national crisis, the central authorities have high expectations. Since most of the Jingwu project has been completed, they were urged to continue to work hard and it was decided to hold the opening ceremony for the Jingwu section on March 12, the anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen. After resting at the Wujiangkou Station in Wuhu, Zhang, accompanied by key officials from various districts, inspected the Wusun section in the original car. In Xuancheng, he met with Zhou Qunnan, the administrative commissioner of the Ninth District, and inquired about the order in southern Anhui and the lives of the people after the elimination of the remaining bandits. He returned to Wuhu at 4:00 PM and transferred to a car back to Beijing (13th).

Secret Copies of Palace Dramas 107

Completely Burned Due to Carelessness by the Drama School

The Palace's Stage Properties and Costumes Also Suffered

Beiping Correspondence: After the Qing Dynasty was overthrown, the palace's collection of theatrical costumes, stage properties, and scenery (such as the scenery in the "Dou Nu Gong Hun Yuan He" play) totaled about 300 boxes. Before the 10th year of the Republic of China, more than 100 boxes of the Qing Palace still existed and were exhibited from time to time. In addition to some of them being purchased by Mei Lanfang, Shang Xiaoyun, and others later, most of them were obtained by the Drama School. Jiao Juyin, the principal of the Drama School, was the nephew of Li Shizeng and had connections with the education circles of Beijing and Tianjin and various aspects of the Forbidden City. Jiao obtained about 50 or 60 of the more than 100 secret copies of palace dramas. These 50 or 60 secret copies of dramas included full plays and legends, some of which were Ming Dynasty manuscripts. These were extremely rare and could not be obtained even by Cheng Changgeng and Tan Xinpei in the past 100 years, so their value is evident.

The Drama School has been established by Jiao for several years and has achieved good results. It has produced many talents. In recent years, it has performed in various theaters in Beijing and gradually won the welcome of general opera fans. The only old-style opera troupe in Beijing, the Faliancheng Society, is already being overwhelmed. Last night (14th), due to a short circuit, a fire suddenly broke out in the school's warehouse. All the costumes, stage properties, and other items were not rescued at all, and the 50 or 60 secret copies of the Qing Palace's unique dramas were also destroyed in the fire. Although the school's property is said to have only suffered a loss of more than 10,000 yuan, the loss in terms of national heritage, documents, and academics is far more than tens of thousands of yuan! Some people say that the original copies of several legends such as "The Peony Pavilion" were also among those burned, which is truly a rare catastrophe for the literary and artistic circles.

In addition to running the Drama School, Jiao also took over the "Zhixingcheng" troupe, which was newly established the year before last but suffered heavy losses and was bought by Jiao last year. The entire troupe has about 60 or 70 students. After Jiao reorganized it, it was moved to the school outside Chongwen Gate, where everything is taught. The academic year is tentatively set for six years, and after graduation, they will join the Drama School and perform together in various places. It is a pity that the fire will undoubtedly affect its future (15th).

Directing the Huai River Project Office to Recruit Merchants to Contract Excavation Work 108

Employing 40,000 Strong Laborers Organized into Forty Teams

Ability to Recruit 1,000 Laborers Suffices for One Team

Zhenjiang Report: The Jiangsu Provincial Project for Directing the Huai River into the Sea stipulates a total workforce of 165,000 people, engaging in micro-labor in twelve counties including Huaiyin and Huaian. The payment in lieu of labor will be handled uniformly by the Huai River into the Sea Project Office. Currently, the office plans to employ 40,000 strong laborers with sound physiques and proficient in construction work, organized into forty teams, to excavate earth. Special recruitment of merchants to contract the work is announced, with the results to be revealed on March 6th. The project overview and contracting methods are as follows:

Project Overview: (1) Work Section: Roughly extends eastward from the vicinity of Lianshui City to Taozikou. Apart from the compulsory labor portion, intermittent sections will be excavated using contracted labor. The work section is approximately located in areas such as Gutan, Lianshui City, Tongying, Zhoumen, Sanwengu, and Taozikou. Starting and stopping points will be designated separately. (2) Soil Quality: The soil consists of alternating layers of soil and sand, with sand being the predominant component. Occasional occurrences of mud and drifting silt exist. (3) Standard Cross-Section: The net width of the riverbed is 35 meters, with an average excavation depth of 8 meters. The excavation depth in the cutting beach portion is 11 meters. The left and right side slopes have a ratio of 1:2.5. The average distance for earth removal is 100 to 150 meters, to be piled into earthen embankments without additional reinforcement. (4) Earthwork: The total length of the seven small sections is approximately 34 kilometers, with an estimated volume of 15 million cubic meters. Each team of 1,000 people is expected to excavate 40,000 cubic meters as the standard. (5) Deadline: From the date of commencement of work, the deadline for completion is May 31st, 1936.

Contracting Methods: (1) According to the work team organization of this office, those who can recruit a team of 1,000 laborers can contract a small section of the project. Those willing to contract more are welcome. (2) Work sheds will be provided by this office, according to regulations of 25 people per shed, with materials issued. Contractors are responsible for transporting, erecting, and maintaining them, and returning them upon completion of the work. (3) Travel expenses to and from the work site, all tools, cooking utensils, bedding, and water-draining equipment for the laborers are to be provided by the contractor. (4) Large accumulations of water will be handled by the drainage stations set up by this office. Localized accumulations of water in the earthen ditches should be cleared by the laborers without additional compensation. (5) The depth of excavation and completion of work for each work section must be in accordance with the regulations of this office. The price per cubic meter is determined by layer as follows: A. The top layer, from the average beach surface down to a depth of 2 meters, is priced at 22 cents of silver per cubic meter. B. The middle layer, from 2 meters to 5 meters, is priced at 25 cents of silver per cubic meter. C. The lower layer, from 5 meters to 8 meters, is priced at 27 cents of silver per cubic meter. D. The bottom layer, from 8 meters to the new riverbed, is priced at 32 cents of silver per cubic meter. (6) The contractor is responsible for the management, food, lodging, and hygiene of the laborers. Site security will be the responsibility of the security team of this office. (7) The contractor's management fee will be issued at a rate of a certain percentage of the total volume price. (8) Laborers' wages will be issued at approximately 80% on a weekly basis, with the balance settled after the total volume is received upon completion of all work. (9) When necessary for wage disbursement, grain coupons may be used to purchase various grains from the grain stations of this office. (10) After the contract is established, no additional price per cubic meter may be requested due to weather conditions or any obstacles in the project. (11) Once the work section is designated, excavation must continue to the specified river channel depth and must not be stopped midway or request a change of work section. (18th)

Songjiang 109

Red Cross Branch Sends Letter to County Magistrate Jin Requesting Guidance on Disaster Relief Methods

The Songjiang branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society, recognizing that since the end of the old lunar year, disaster victims from western Zhejiang have been flocking to Songjiang, begging for food along the way, and fearing that this would disrupt public order, and for the sake of providing relief for disaster victims' clothing, food, childbirth, illness, and death, immediately established a refugee shelter to engage in receiving them, as has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Now we record the resolutions of its yesterday's meeting and its official letter to the county government below. (1) Resolutions: The 9th meeting was held at 2:00 PM on February 17th, chaired by Sheng Jingsheng, with more than 20 attendees. (Item 1) A letter to the county government requesting attendance to provide guidance on public security measures was resolved as follows: After this society established the shelter, it completely accommodated the disaster victims in Songjiang. However, those begging on the streets are still occasionally seen. There are two reasons for this: 1. Philanthropists in Songjiang provide separate distributions, unable to act in unity. Refugees seek sustenance wherever they can, making it difficult to get them to go to the shelter. 2. Watchmen are needed for the refugees' boats. Disaster victims cannot be kept together in the shelter. There are still those passing through who beg along the streets. The members of this society find it difficult to resolve the above difficulties. The county magistrate is responsible for public security and should be invited to attend to provide guidance, so as to achieve perfection. (Item 2) A request for members to raise funds was resolved as follows: The chairman of the board, Zhou Xuewen, will prepare a donation booklet to be distributed to each member for fundraising at any time, and all institutions are requested to assist. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM. (2) Official Letter: Respected Sir, At the 9th meeting of this society on February 17th, the most difficult aspect of the Zhejiang disaster refugee shelter is that many refugees entering the shelter still go out to beg. The underlying reasons are approximately threefold: 1. Philanthropists in Songjiang provide separate distributions of money and rice, unable to act in unity. Disaster victims harbor the mentality that more is better, making it difficult to prohibit them from seeking elsewhere. 2. Watchmen are needed for the refugees' boats. Disaster victims cannot be kept together in the shelter. 3. It is impossible to investigate refugees passing through and begging along the way. The above three points were discussed and it was agreed that this society established the shelter with the original intention of completely accommodating disaster victims in Songjiang to avoid them begging along the way, which would disrupt public order. Now that there are the above-mentioned difficulties, the members of this society find it difficult to resolve them. The county magistrate, as the leader of the county, is responsible for public security and should be invited to attend to provide guidance, so as to achieve perfection, etc., as recorded in the minutes. This society has now decided to convene officials of this society at 2:00 PM on February 21st at the office of this society (inside the St. Joseph's Hospital) to discuss relief measures. At that time, we respectfully request your presence for guidance, to supplement our shortcomings. Sincerely, To: Jin, County Magistrate of Songjiang, From: Zhu Jiuwang, President of the Songjiang Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society; Sheng Yuanyin, Speaker; Zhou Xuewen, Chairman of the Board.

Bandit Wu Shusheng Handed Over to Court

Wu Shusheng, a notorious bandit from Punan Shanyang, also known as Little Ah San, now renamed Wu Suisheng, was wanted by Zhejiang. On the night of December 27th last year, he ambushed the back door of Yang Xiangjin's house. When Yang went out to urinate, Wu suspected him of being a poor thief, so he stabbed Yang in the right leg with a knife. Yang shouted for help, and neighbors heard the sound and helped to tie Wu up. He was handed over to the Shanyang Security Detachment and then transferred to the brigade headquarters for interrogation. Yesterday, he was transferred to the court prosecutor's office for investigation and legal action.

Frustrated by Marital Discord, Wife Cuts Off Genitals and Hangs Self

A peasant woman named Pan, residing outside the Xu Gate at the Shanren Bridge, had an adopted son named Qiaoquan, 28 years old. He married Jinzhu, daughter of Xu Shuqing. The couple had marital discord. The night before last, Jinzhu returned to her parents' home. Qiaoquan went alone to his in-laws' house, cut off his genitals, and hanged himself. His mother heard the news and rushed to mourn over the body, picking up the severed parts and preserving them. Currently, the relevant parties have been sent to the police station for investigation. Yesterday (18th), the local court went to examine the body. The case is very strange and unusual.

Two Robberies Occur Outside the West Gate

The Wu County Public Security Bureau reported on the 17th, according to Tang Renjie, the patrol officer of the First Sub-station outside the West Gate, that Zhou Yibao's home in Dongtang Township within the jurisdiction of the sub-station was robbed by bandits, who looted a self-defense Type 79 short-barreled rifle, as well as foreign clothing and other items. Zhou Yibao was also beaten on the head, lost consciousness, and fell to the ground. The director of the bureau, Xu Baoguang, is conducting a strict interrogation because the case involves robbery. He reported it to the First Public Security Sub-station for investigation. The county magistrate, upon hearing the news, went to the First Sub-station on the 17th to inquire and ordered patrol officer Tang to quickly purchase threads and arrest the bandits in order to ensure local peace.

Jiangyin 113

Levying Boat Taxes to Dredge River Ports

The county government held a committee meeting on the 16th to discuss the dredging of the Huangchugang South Canal. Regarding the funding issue, in addition to the provincial assistance of 65,000 yuan, there is still a shortfall of 95,000 yuan. It was decided to request approval from the provincial authorities to retain all the dredging fees collected in the county, and to use the road construction mu tax, the original water conservancy fee collection, and the 50,000 yuan face value of Jiangsu construction bonds as collateral to borrow from a consortium. Starting from July of this year, collection points for dredging fees will be set up at Huangtiangang and Sihe Gate, with a term of three years. The loan will be repaid monthly by the Economic Committee to the consortium from January 1936. The recorded dredging fees and boat tax collection orders are as follows: Cargo ships, salt ships, yellow croaker ships, included within, less than 100 dan, collect one yuan per ship; more than 100 dan, collect 5 jiao per 15 dan. Log rafts, with a length of seven chi and a width of four zhang, collect two yuan per raft. Bamboo rafts, with a length of seven chi and a width of three zhang, collect two yuan per raft. If the excess is less than one raft, it will be calculated as one raft. Bamboo cargo ships, regardless of the load, collect one yuan per ship. Pig ships collect 3 fen per pig. Reed boats collect one yuan per boat. Coal ships collect 2 jiao per 10 tons. If it is less than 10 tons, it will also be calculated as 10 tons. Cargo barges, regardless of the load, collect 2 jiao. Empty ships entering and exiting, and small barges registered in this port, are limited to not leaving Huangtiangang and Sihe Gate. Empty boats from Jiangbei, Huangshi ships produced in Sen County, coffin-carrying ships, and ash and manure ships are exempt from fees.

Gaoyou 114

Fire in Xiaji River Burns One Child to Death

In the home of farmer Ge Damo in Xiaji River, Fifth District of this county, at around 9:00 PM last night (15th), his wife was careless while cooking dinner, igniting the accumulated firewood, which suddenly caused a fire. Flames immediately burst through the roof, and the fire illuminated the sky. The alarm bell was immediately rung, and villagers rushed to put out the fire, but the fire was too fierce and could not be extinguished. The fire also spread to the homes of neighbors Zhu Dexi, Xia Er, and Xia Baocai. The fire was finally extinguished at around 1:00 AM, with more than 30 rooms in total from the four families, as well as clothing and utensils, all reduced to ashes, with losses totaling over a thousand yuan. Zhu's four-year-old daughter was sleeping in bed and could not be rescued, resulting in her tragic death in the fire.

Local News

Ministry of Finance Encourages Foreign Bank Inflow 120

Future Re-exports to be Exempt from Taxes

Yesterday, the Director-General of Customs was Instructed to Comply

The Ministry of Finance, upon receiving petitions from the All-China Federation of Commerce and other organizations, regarding promoting foreign bank inflows to regulate the market for the sake of invigorating finance and developing industry and commerce, has now stipulated three measures. Yesterday, a special instruction was issued to the Director-General of Customs, scheduled to be implemented on the 19th (today). The original text of the instruction and the reply to the All-China Federation of Commerce and other organizations are recorded below:

Ministry of Finance Instruction to the Director-General of Customs

Instruction No. 12 (Shanghai Money): Order to the Director-General of Customs: In the case of the joint petition from the All-China Federation of Commerce, the Shanghai Banking Association, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the Shanghai Money Industry Association, requesting the encouragement of foreign bank inflows to regulate the market, it is noted that these associations, recognizing that the export of silver has been increasing daily, causing hardship for domestic industry and commerce, petitioned and were granted a decree by the Ministry to levy a silver export equalization tax. Since then, exports have gradually decreased, people's confidence has been somewhat restored, and the national economy and people's livelihoods have benefited. However, the key to finance is circulation. The purpose of the equalization tax is to restrict the export of silver, but it is also sufficient to restrict the inflow of foreign bank funds. Under current market conditions, there is a possibility of gradually returning foreign silver, but due to the silver tax, they are hesitant. We request that you, in the spirit of maintaining industrial and commercial activity and finance, clearly stipulate measures to encourage the import of foreign silver, ordering the Director-General of Customs to allow registration with customs for all foreign silver imported from abroad. In the future, when re-exported, it will be exempt from all principal and surtaxes. In this way, foreign silver can be expected to be imported at any time to meet domestic needs. Moreover, the import of silver is not included in the domestic silver reserves, and granting tax exemption upon re-export is not inconsistent with the original purpose of the Ministry's taxation. Therefore, we respectfully request your approval for implementation. The Foreign Exchange Market Stabilization Committee has also submitted a similar request to the Ministry. Upon investigation, the addition of a silver export tax and the levying of an equalization tax were originally intended to cope with the crisis and stabilize finance. Since implementation, silver exports have decreased, and the market has been stabilized, benefiting the national economy and people's livelihoods. However, for the sake of invigorating finance and developing industry and commerce, the encouragement of foreign bank inflows requested by the associations is in line with the Ministry's intention and is not inconsistent with the purpose of adding a silver export tax and levying an equalization tax. It should be approved. The following measures are now stipulated: (1) For raw silver or national currency imported from abroad, the amount and date of import shall be registered with the importing customs, which will issue a certificate. In the future, if re-export is necessary, the original importer may present the original certificate to the Ministry to exchange for a tax-exempt passport for the original amount of raw silver or national currency. (2) Those holding the aforementioned tax-exempt passport for export, in addition to paying a 2.25% tax, will be exempt from the silver export tax and equalization tax added on October 15, 1934. (3) The minimum amount of raw silver imported each time shall not be less than 500,000 ounces. If it is national currency, it shall be converted and calculated accordingly. In addition to the instruction, this order is to inform the Director-General of Customs to comply, to be announced and implemented on February 19th, and to report to the Ministry for record after issuing the certificate. This order.

Ministry of Finance Reply to the All-China Federation of Commerce and Others

Ministry of Finance Reply to the All-China Federation of Commerce, the Shanghai Banking Association, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the Shanghai Money Industry Association, regarding the petition to encourage foreign silver imports to regulate the market. According to the joint petition from the associations, requesting a clear stipulation of measures to encourage the import of foreign silver, ordering the Director-General of Customs to allow registration with customs for foreign silver imported from abroad, and exempting principal and surtaxes upon re-export in the future, to regulate the market, and the Foreign Exchange Market Stabilization Committee also submitted a similar request. All have been read. Upon investigation, the addition of a silver export tax and the levying of an equalization tax were originally intended to cope with the crisis and stabilize finance. Since implementation, silver exports have decreased, and the market has been stabilized, benefiting the national economy and people's livelihoods. However, for the sake of invigorating finance and developing industry and commerce, the encouragement of foreign bank inflows requested by the associations is in line with the Ministry's intention and is not inconsistent with the purpose of adding a silver export tax and levying an equalization tax. It should be approved. The following measures are now stipulated: (1) For raw silver or national currency imported from abroad, the amount and date of import shall be registered with the importing customs, which will issue a certificate. In the future, if re-export is necessary, the original importer may present the original certificate to the Ministry to exchange for a tax-exempt passport for the original amount of raw silver or national currency. (2) Those holding the aforementioned tax-exempt passport for export, in addition to paying a 2.25% tax, will be exempt from the silver export tax and equalization tax added on October 15, 1934. (3) The minimum amount of raw silver imported each time shall not be less than 500,000 ounces. If it is national currency, it shall be converted and calculated accordingly. In addition to ordering the Director-General of Customs to comply and announce and implement it on February 19th, this reply is to inform you for your information. This reply.
