Page 22

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Talk About Secrets 218

— Jue Fu

Children, I can play with a kaleidoscope with great interest, reluctant to put it down; villagers, when they encounter someone performing magic, will stop and watch intently. If the kaleidoscope is taken apart and it is known that it is originally composed of a few colored plastic sheets and a few pieces of glass; if the principles of magic are all understood, and it is known that many of the changes are merely due to skillful techniques: the kaleidoscope will be thrown away from the child's hand, and magic will no longer be able to attract passersby. The reason why these two things are valued is because of their secrets.

Children find everything fun, no matter what they encounter; country bumpkins find everything in the city interesting, precisely because they do not understand the secrets within various things.

A taciturn person often evokes admiration and awe; he is unwilling to reveal the secrets in his heart, making himself seem unfathomable, which is also a reason.

The reason why humanity can be passed down from generation to generation, never feeling tired or stagnant, is said to be because life itself is a great mystery, and the secrets of the universe can never be completely deciphered, which may also be a reason: if all the things in the universe are understood, and the ultimate meaning of life is completely clear, perhaps humanity would become extinct.

The function of secrets is so worthy of praise!

We Chinese deeply understand this principle, and our utilization of secrets is far superior to others. This can be seen simply by looking at our compatriots' consistent way of handling affairs, not emphasizing analysis, not paying attention to logic, but only relying on intuition and speculation, vaguely glossing over matters.

In recent years, is "open secret" not a very fashionable term? This is also because some of our compatriots have recognized the greatness of the function of secrets, so even matters that are originally public are made to carry a bit of mystery.

Unwilling to unravel the secrets of matters, but only making superficial observations, is indeed our cleverness: because in this way, we can save ourselves a lot of trouble and enjoy a lot of immediate joy. However, as a result, while others have evolved to the point of soaring in the sky, we are still stagnating in an era of using feet as transportation, which is still a shortcoming!

Fishing Boat 219

— Ya Fei

It was an evening approaching darkness; the northwest wind was blowing in the sky, and a setting sun from the west was blown colorless, as if it was about to fall.

The bare branches on the old mulberry tree howled in the wind; not a single bird could be found in the surrounding area.

In the corner of Taihu Lake, a long stone embankment stretched out, sheltering many fishing boats, one, two, three... crowded together. — Chacha — chacha — the sound of sharpening hooks, and — huh — huh — the sound of mending nets echoed each other. The fishing boats could not withstand the waves, drifting on the water like leaves; the masts on several cargo boats also swayed in the air, while the boatmen hid in the cabins.

"Gengsheng, we have to set sail earlier today; with such a strong wind, there will surely be good business," Guisheng said to the person on the boat next door while sharpening his hooks.

"I think the wind on the outer lake is too strong today; we can't go to Miaoshan Dike. It's better to check the situation at Xiwang Bay. It's fine for you to go to Ziwan Bay," Gengsheng replied, puffing on his pipe, looking at the sky with experience.

"Yes, there are several fish nests there, and since the planting— until now, we haven't even recovered the capital!"

"One year of heavy rain, one year of drought, the fish in Taihu Lake, those that escape, those that are caught, maybe in two or three years, even the fish fry will be gone! This year is really terrible. The fishery tax from last winter is still owed. There was no snow in winter, but spring snow keeps falling. It looks like it won't be a good year! Sigh!"

"The heavens want to play tricks on us poor people. There's no way. We still have to live. Besides this broken fishing boat and that net, we can't find another way to survive. Moreover, my family's rice for tomorrow's breakfast is still on the hook. Tonight, we should eat dinner early and go out and try our luck!" Guisheng finished speaking and lowered his head to sharpen his hooks.

Both of them were silent for a long time, except for the sound of sharpening hooks, mending nets, and the whistling north wind, everything else was silent, as silent as death.

Darkness crept into the human world; the entire nature was ruled by darkness; there was no moon or stars in the sky, but the wind was even more rampant than before.

Not a single fishing boat could be seen in that corner; on the dark lake surface, only scattered fishing lights appeared, swaying up and down.

At that time, Guisheng was squatting on the bow of the boat, using his skilled and experienced night eyes, watching the movement of the water. He held his breath, not even daring to breathe. The boy shaking the boat was always following Guisheng's instructions, rowing back and forth. Because the tattered cotton coat on his body was not enough to keep out the cold, his body was shivering like chaff.

Rowing along an arc-shaped bay around Yashan, the shadows of Dalongtou and Xiaolongtou mountains were still faintly visible. Guisheng tightly held the net rope, and his body couldn't help but shiver. The waves hit the boat, agitating the small boat like a startled animal, almost knocking Guisheng off the bow.

"Damn it, the wind is too strong, I can't hold on, there's no hope!" He gasped!

Strings of water droplets flew on the edge of his broken felt hat, forming icicles; even his tattered cotton coat was covered with ice spots. He could no longer struggle in such a cold wind; all the blood in his body had frozen, and he had lost all sensation in his hands and feet. He hurriedly pulled up the net and threw it into the boat; it was so heavy, but the "plop!" sound didn't sound like fish. He examined it and saw pieces of ice hanging on the net rope, bright and shining. There was only one fish, weighing no more than three or two taels. He checked the small harpoon and found a small fish the size of a holly leaf. He sighed and said nothing; the boat boy, without strength, rowed the boat into the corner, but the sky was already the color of a fish's belly!

Winter at Xuanwu Lake 220

— Zong Xin

Stone City, formerly a famous scenic spot in Jiangnan during the Six Dynasties, is now Kyoto. In people's imagination, there are beautiful mountains and rivers, and famous historical sites. One should take a trip to Nanjing!

People living a wandering life in the big city, the sound of machines, the gas of cars, have felt particularly tired, dragging the gray life of the cross of thousands of pounds of life, even more want to escape to the beautiful mountains, lakeside, to relax. Then, the head of Stone City seems to be swaying in my mind.

Holding a jumping heart, I was intercepted by the train like a long snake crawling into the bottom of Stone City, the desolate mountains and piles on the edge of the city, the old city walls, although indifferent, also have a bit of high spirit. This is the famous Stone City!

However, living in the city, I feel that: other than being more deserted than Shanghai, there is nothing to relieve boredom. It is so mediocre, leaving behind the thick old Chinese sentiment.

Going to the First Park, unintentionally walking along a city river like a shit ditch, a friend pointed to the black water below and said: "This is the Qinhuai River!" I was a little surprised: "Is this the beautiful and charming Qinhuai River?" Ah, there is no pleasant singing, some small boats on the river are quietly lying there, vaguely flashing some tattered figures.

Not very interested, the heart to visit the famous city. Bored at a friend's house, feeling extremely bored. I remembered reading an article about the autumn of Xuanwu, which aroused my interest, and I went to Xuanwu Lake. Now it is winter, what kind of appearance does Xuanwu Lake have!

Arriving at the edge of Xuanwu Gate, looking up at the high city head, my heart could not help but beat faster. Beautiful Xuanwu Lake, a haggard and dry person's heart, will immediately be immersed in your embrace. I am pre-rich, that joyful kindness when dissipating infinite troubles. I love the beautiful scenery by the lake the most!

Slowly, with a look of complete indulgence, I walked out of Xuanwu Gate. Looking around, the leafless willows hung down withered, as indifferent as my gray mood, and my heart gradually calmed down. Looking closely, the sides of the dirt road are full of these decaying willows. Under the willows are decorated with a few vendors selling peanuts and the like. The tourists are so scattered, I can't see a noble person wearing fashionable clothes, only a few passersby!

Before the small hillocks of Xuanwu Gate unfolded to the east, a few short houses were scattered, so desolate and quiet, a friend raised his finger and said: "I often fantasize about renting a small house here, but it is really too desolate!"

I looked at the lake water under the city, which was not blue, and the gray-black leaves floating everywhere. It was a bit frozen, not obvious, I thought to myself: this is Xuanwu Lake! It's just a vague sense of cold. But I still wanted to find some scenery to relieve my boredom on the desolate and cold Xuanwu Lake. Chao Ji was pointing his finger and saying. "You don't know, Xuanwu Lake does have its merits, but unfortunately it is winter. In spring, summer, and autumn, the willows on both sides are green, hanging down so elegantly, and the lake is full of lotus flowers blooming. Boating on the lake with two or three tourists is quite interesting!"

But now the lake is just full of stagnant water, scattered with many dead leaves. Not a single boat is floating on the lake, although the boat owners by the lake are greeting us, saying that for only twenty copper plates, we can go around the lake once and come back, but we did not pay attention to them.

Walking along the lake, the desolate heart is still desolate, the dead leaves on the lake are scattered all over the vast lake surface, we can only talk to each other, it is already desolate, let's go back! Facing Xuanwu Gate, we entered the city. I felt like I hadn't been to Xuanwu at all. Famous city is also. I still feel very strange! It's like I haven't visited Stone City at all.

Hero 221

— Jiang Ye

"Friend: Stop crying, even if you die, in twenty years, you will be a great man again."

His companions called him Lao Li from Shandong, but he was still a stubborn person. He had been locked in this wooden cage for more than ten days, and he had never seen him unhappy; he spent his days talking about happy stories with his companions, and his blood-red face always had a smiling expression. Now, he was a little saddened by the crying of the companion who had just been locked in this morning. The more impatient he became, the more afraid he was of hearing the sobbing cries, he suppressed the fire of anger in his heart, walked to the side of the crying companion, patted him on the shoulder and said.

That companion, since coming here this morning, had not eaten a single meal, but only hid on the wooden bed or stood by the wooden railing crying. This not only made the Shandong fellow and all the companions in the cell uneasy, but even the people in the surrounding cells became impatient. Originally, no one would think about other things, but just talked and laughed all day long, but because of him, everyone's heart could no longer be at peace.

The Shandong fellow was more anxious than anyone else, and his flushed face became even redder. Seeing that all the people in the cell were ruined by the companion's crying, he felt angry in his heart, not thinking about himself: a person who has lived to be twenty or thirty years old is still like a woman, even if it is a big deal, he can think about it secretly, always crying like this, will the official give you a way out? There really are such fools in the world!

The more the Shandong fellow thought about it, the more ridiculous he felt, the more he saw the companion crying harder, the more he felt his own greatness. Indeed, the Shandong fellow was a hero, he often said to his companions:

"I have been living alone outside since I was sixteen years old, I have done everything, I have enjoyed all the happiness, and I have suffered all the hardships, so what is jail, just die! Hmph, in twenty years I will be a great man again, what is there to be afraid of, don't think too little of yourself!"

This heroic thought of his, almost everyone in the cell was infected by him a little. Whenever he talked about his past life, what he had done in the past, he would smile. Since he was locked in this cage, all the companions here were happy to chat with him, even those who did odd jobs outside liked to listen to his stories.

But since this morning, he has been very unhappy because the companion cried too much. Although he was angry that the companion shouldn't cry, his deep heart was also a little sad. He didn't say a word all day, and he inadvertently turned to his own unhappy thoughts.

The daytime in winter is very short. Suddenly, it became naturally dark, and although the companion was already crying and only sobbing, his heart was even more sad. He stared blankly at the dark sky, spacing out.

When distributing the blankets, the Shandong fellow always joked with the old man. But tonight, he sat motionless in that corner, silent. After the old man left, he grabbed an iron-like blanket, and lay down with a few people from Guangdong. At this time, the people in the cell were talking and laughing about him in a chaotic way. He silently burrowed into the bedding, even his breathing was very low.

He was thinking, thinking that this time he would definitely lose his life, and he also thought of his family, wife, son, and old mother. He thought of his whole life, and he also thought of his encounter that would explode in front of him soon. He felt terrible in his heart, and his heart became as cold as ice. It seemed that the death god's poisonous whip was whipping his brave ambition.

The sound of crying sounded in his ears again, he opened his eyes and stared hatefully at the crying companion. That icy heart was burning with the heat of life again. He knew he couldn't be so fragile. He should be a hero, he shouted loudly to that companion:

"Friend: Stop crying, even if you die, in twenty years you will be a great man again."

Boring Days 222

— Simon

It is not necessarily because of being idle all day long, with empty hands and empty feet, that one feels an overwhelming sense of boredom. Boredom does not really exist in action, but rather in the mind, in things that are too familiar, and in habits that are exhausted. Often when one feels inexplicably bored in the house, one thinks of going out for a stroll, but without a destination, dragging slow steps, the heart is already very bored. Since one is out, one simply follows where the legs lead, wandering aimlessly, not knowing when one will stop, or where one will go. When one comes out, one still holds a faint thought of relieving boredom, but after walking for a while, one's body already feels somewhat tired, so quickly giving up that little thought, only feeling an unspeakable boredom, almost bored to the point where one is too lazy to walk.

The feelings of boredom are most subtle, and at the same time, most illusory. This subtlety and illusion are completely impossible to explain with words, and can only be deeply tasted by oneself. The heart is like stepping on a pile of cotton, swaying remotely; the heart is like a deep, bottomless hole, empty and vast. One cannot sit still, cannot lie still, everything feels dull and rigid. Nothing is exciting. The depravity of the mood has reached its extreme. Lying in bed, thinking of falling asleep for a while, perhaps being able to drive away the boredom, but it is useless. Despite closing one's eyes tightly, one cannot fall asleep, so one becomes more irritable. One climbs up and casually opens a book to flip through, but one cannot read it, after reading a few lines, one throws it away, still bored. Nothing can arouse interest, an endless sense of boredom envelops the entire body and mind. The more one searches for something to play with to eliminate this boredom, the more serious the boredom becomes.

Usually, there are many ways to pass the time that one likes, or things that one has a considerable interest in. But now, that doesn't work either. Thinking about them gives me a headache; those things have completely lost the interest they used to give me.

I am almost so anxious that I want to groan out loud. Boredom has simply become a painful symptom. Locked in the house, pacing back and forth endlessly, a person is as if the heart has been drawn out. After walking for a long time, if the steps one has taken are connected, one really doesn't know how far it is. But other than adding to the heavy feeling of boredom, there is nothing else. When busy with work and rest, as soon as the sky dawns, one buries oneself at the desk, and the day's tasks have not been properly sorted out, and in the blink of an eye, the sky has darkened. At such times, one will often unconsciously sigh towards the setting sun in the west: why does time pass so quickly? But when bored, although time also passes quickly, one still thinks that time is passing too slowly.

I have suffered enough from the torment of boredom. If one says that the reason for having a sense of boredom is always because one is full all day long, and has nothing to do, then that is not the case. Every day, there are really many things I should do, I am only afraid of not being able to do them completely, naturally there is no leisure. Already having so many tasks entangled, one should be busy in body and mind, so why do I always complain of boredom? This is confusing even to myself. I can't think of a real reason, perhaps it is mostly due to the fact that although there are things to do, certain things originally have a certain passion and meaning, but as time goes by, perseverance gradually fades, fading to the point of completely disappearing, and the meaning of certain things themselves also perishes.

School Teacher 223

— Jiang Tian

It was getting dark, and the withered branches on both sides of the road were being blown east and west by the north wind, making noise. This quiet Huiai East Road was even quieter.

Old Wang, with two textbooks and a student's paper wrapped in his arms, was walking along the road listlessly.

"Old Wang: Where are you going? Did you get your salary today?"

Mr. Li walked up behind Old Wang, patted him on the shoulder and asked. At this moment, Old Wang was thinking about the salary matter, and Mr. Li's question made him feel angry. He stared at Mr. Li with his round eyes and said:

"Old Li, don't mention it. Not only didn't I get it today, but I also got a scolding. Damn it, this is really not something a human should do. Teaching only leads to starvation!"

"Old Wang, is it just you who gets scolded, aren't other people the same? I also don't want to do this job, but... I can't find anything else to do."

Page 23

"Old friend; you're still okay, but I'm in trouble! My wife is seriously ill at home, and I'm not feeling well myself. Damn it, they don't pay my salary, they already owe me five months! I can't get a single penny."

When Old Wang thought of his wife, he felt even angrier. His heart was numb with anger. He looked at Mr. Li, lowered his head, and didn't say a word.

"Old friend; don't worry too much, we're just unlucky. Let's find something else to do! This is a very hard way to make a living. Goodbye!"

Mr. Li waved to him as he spoke, and walked into a dark alley. Old Wang shook his head, sighed, and walked home.

"Damn it, I'm coming back empty-handed again today, what will my wife do?"

As soon as Old Wang stepped into the door, he seemed to have no strength in his feet as he walked upstairs, thinking about this in his heart.

Old Wang ran into the room, put down the textbooks and student papers, and walked to his wife's bedside. Her face was pale, she was breathing weakly, and her eyes were deeply sunken. Tears seemed to be hanging in her deep eye sockets. When Old Wang saw his wife's appearance at this time, he felt even more anger in his heart. He held her thin hand and cursed in his heart:

"Damn it, everything is because of not having money, five months without pay?"

His wife opened her deeply sunken eyes, and tears rolled down from her eye sockets, looking at him, speaking very weakly, almost inaudible. When he heard these words, he felt even more sad. A shadow of grief and sorrow tightly covered his heart. He felt his breathing was suffocating, and he felt that all the misery in the world was unbearable. At this moment, he thought of the golden age of the past, the happiness of love, his deceased parents, and his younger brother who went to teach in Nanyang. He thought of everything in the past. A wave of dizziness came over him, and the room seemed to be spinning...

Shanghai Shenbao Supplement Architecture Weekly

Analysis of "Force" in Ancient Chinese Architecture 228

— Xi Hao

China has exerted great effort in promoting architecture throughout the dynasties. From the Qin and Han dynasties to the Song and Yuan dynasties, exquisite buildings that dominated the world were continuously produced. In today's metropolises, we can still find traces of them. Although they have been battered by wind and rain for thousands or hundreds of years, they still stand majestically. We can imagine the solidity and durability of this oriental architecture.

Another aspect of oriental architecture that is most satisfying is its "color." Foreigners call it "oriental color." Its delicate and appropriate arrangement cannot be compared to any other building in the world. We can observe this from the palaces and temples left behind by previous dynasties.

Our ancient architecture was so exquisite and solid, why are we gradually neglecting it now and striving to adopt Western methods? There is indeed a big problem here—the problem of "force."

If we quietly observe the structure of the ancient palaces and temples that still exist today with scientific eyes, we can discover that the force on each pillar and beam is "compressive force." Because we did not have steel as a building material in the past, the wood used was very thick, making the entire building solid. The more solid the building, the thicker the wood used. In this way, the "compressive force" on each piece of wood greatly increased. This huge compressive force only allows for horizontal development of general buildings and does not allow for vertical development. Therefore, most ancient Chinese buildings have wide halls and courtyards, but few have high-rise buildings with dozens of floors. This type of building would absolutely not exist in the twenty-first century city where land is worth its weight in gold.

The structure of modern buildings not only has compressive force but also tensile force and other forces. Sometimes several forces are mixed together, resulting in mutual cancellation. In this way, the force that each unit can withstand increases, and the number of floors of the building can be increased as much as possible. Just look at the lightweight steel frames of modern times, which majestically support dozens of floors of concrete buildings without the slightest danger. This is the result of being able to make ingenious use of "force."

Ancient architects did not seem to pay attention to the use of tensile force. In fact, the tensile force of wood is extremely weak, and even if it is used, there is a risk of fracture!

In addition to the compressive force on the wood, each square brick in ancient buildings is subjected to huge compressive force. They all bear considerable responsibility for supporting the entire building. In this way, the increase in the weight of the bricks hinders the construction of multi-story buildings, which is another fatal flaw in ancient architecture.

In short, the failure to skillfully apply the distribution of "force" in ancient Chinese architecture is probably the main reason for its gradual decline!

A General Overview of Shanghai Construction in the Past Year (II) 229

— Yang Dehui

In the French Concession, the total value of construction in October of last year was 10,841,000 yuan. The prosperity of construction in January and February was unparalleled, almost tripling compared to the same period in the 22nd year of the Republic. January was 925,000 yuan, and February was 1,045,000 yuan, and most of the buildings were grand apartment projects, hence such value. In particular, the 14-story apartment at the corner of Route Petain and Route Wenhlin was worth several million yuan. There were also several 8- and 9-story buildings. The construction value in March was 2,924,000 yuan, and in April was 1,361,000 yuan. The value in May was relatively low, only 771,000 yuan, and in June it was 805,150 yuan. In these six months, a total of 7,831,150 yuan was spent. Although the value in May and June was low, it was still 190% higher than the same period in the 22nd year of the Republic. If we classify the buildings, there were 25 apartments, 133 Western-style houses, 48 semi-Western-style halls, 324 Chinese-style residences, 83 stores, 7 factories, 4 schools, and 48 other buildings. The total value of construction in July and August was 2,450,000 yuan. In these two months, the weather was extremely hot, but the value of construction increased compared to May and June. This is a sign of the booming construction in the French Concession in recent years. There were 72 Western-style halls, 80 semi-Western-style halls, and 64 Chinese-style residences. Among them, the large-scale projects were the French Police Station, worth 150,000 yuan, and two hospitals, worth more than 500,000 yuan in total. If we average the construction value of these eight months, it is about 1,250,000 yuan per month. However, in September, it plummeted to 383,000 yuan, and in October, it fell further to 176,500 yuan. This is not a surprising fact. We know that population and construction are originally linked. The population of the French Concession only increased to 0.33% last year, compared to 4.94% in the 20th and 21st years of the Republic, and 3.75% in the 21st and 22nd years of the Republic, a difference of ten times! Because of this, most of the Chinese-style housing constructed in the French Concession last year, apart from the grand apartment buildings, was renovated from old halls. We can see that the western part of the concession is full of tall apartment buildings, which shows the recent construction trend in the French Concession. This type of apartment building is suitable for the needs of general residents in Shanghai, so it is a very developed type of construction, and it can also be said to be an aspiration for a garden city (to be continued).

Steel and its Protection Methods (Continued) 230

— Qin

To meet the first requirement, architects have used a type of steel material called "metallic wood," which is made by cold-rolling or bending flat steel sheets or strips. It has great strength in construction. It is used as studs, panels, etc., and flanges are used to increase its strength. There have been many improvements recently. Regarding joints, there are two points: one is the joint between steel materials, and the other is the joint between steel materials and other objects. The joints between ordinary steels are all made by forging, either by spark type, resistance type, or other various forging methods. The joints between steel and other objects vary depending on the object, and the results of research by engineers have also been improved and varied. How can their types be counted? As for durability, evidence from past facts and experiments shows that the durability of steel is higher than that of other building materials. In dry air, steel can maintain its original state indefinitely. Even under normal circumstances, it is not a problem to maintain it for thirty to forty years. However, attacks by mixtures and corrosion by chemical substances such as acidic vapors can easily shorten its life.

There are three common methods for protecting steel sheets in construction:

(1) Paint protective layer. If we place steel in dry air, its quality will not change even after a hundred years, and it will be as strong as the beginning. This is because the surface of the steel itself has already combined with the oxygen in the air to form an extremely thin layer of oxide, preventing further oxidation. However, under ordinary circumstances, we have to apply paint to protect its surface so that it does not come into contact with water vapor or other harmful substances. Red lead paint is very effective. Other paints, such as those using zinc oxide, lead and chromium compounds, white lead, blue lead, etc. as fillers, can also be used. Before applying the paint, the dust and dirt on the steel surface must be removed to make it dry, and then the paint is applied with a brush or by spraying. According to the results of experiments by American architects, steel sheets coated with red lead paint were still intact after thirty-five years. It can be seen that if steel is properly protected, its durability is extremely high, and it is important to repair cracks or paint peeling off immediately. This paint protection method is commonly used.

(2) Coating protection layer. The light of coating steel surfaces was first achieved by the method of galvanizing. Later, Europeans used magnetic surfaces to protect steel, which was a very good method. Therefore, Americans have also recently started to follow suit. There are several advantages of coating: first, its color can be arbitrarily matched; second, its durability; and third, it is easy to clean. The coating method is to apply a magnetic liquid to the steel surface at a temperature of about 3,000 degrees Fahrenheit. Magnetic materials contain the most sand and boron, so their texture is firm and can prevent the erosion of all water vapor and acids. The magnetic material adheres to the steel surface with great adhesion, and will only fail when the strength of the steel is insufficient. Coated steel sheets are suitable for outdoor and internal edge decoration, and can be made more colorful by adding copper joints.

(3) Resin protective layer. Resin is made artificially, dissolved in a suitable deep liquid, and added with opaque filler, and then applied to the steel surface. This type of protective layer is generally used for those that are urgently needed and must be dried immediately. Its durability is very strong, and it is also used on automobiles, utensils, and gas stations, but its price seems to be more expensive than the other two types.

In addition to those with a protective layer, there are also steel sheets that do not need protection, which is what we usually call stainless steel. Stainless steel contains a small amount of chromium, so under normal circumstances, an extremely thin protective layer of compound is formed on its surface, but it still does not lose its original luster, so it is called stainless steel. Stainless steel has been used more and more widely in recent years, and it also has great potential in construction. By virtue of its strong strength and rust-proof characteristics, it can fulfill both the engineering and aesthetic missions in construction. This is why European and American architects are happy to use it. It is suitable for all steel plates, steel sheets, steel bars, steel pipes, steel wires, steel nails, and cast models. Its future development is truly limitless.

Building Materials Science (II) 231

— Zhu Zhenmu

Section 4: Categories of Building Materials

There are only two categories of materials used in construction: metals and non-metals.

Metallic building materials can be further divided into three types: ferrous metals, non-ferrous metals, and alloys.

(1) Ferrous Metals:

(A) Pig Iron Category:

1. Overview—Pig iron, cast iron, and semi-steel all belong to this category.

2. General Properties—Contains a large amount of carbon. Has a crystalline structure, is hard and brittle, and lacks ductility.

3. Applications—Used for refining wrought iron and steel; also used to make pig iron furniture.

(B) Wrought Iron Category:

1. Overview—Similar to low-grade steel.

2. General Properties—Contains 0.12% carbon. Is highly ductile, can be forge-welded, and is more resistant to rust.

3. Applications—Water pipes and other wrought iron furniture and items.

(C) Steel Category:

1. Overview—Steel is made by mixing and refining iron and carbon, usually containing 1.25% carbon. Other metals can also be added to achieve various effects. (More details will be provided later). Manufacturing methods include the open-hearth process, the Bessemer process, and the electric arc furnace process, which will be discussed in later chapters.

2. General Properties—All types of steel are ductile and melt easily.

3. Applications—Steel skeletons and steel bars are fundamental to construction.

(2) Non-Ferrous Metals:

(A) Copper Category:

1. Overview—Refined from copper ore and made into sheets or wires.

2. General Properties—Extremely high electrical conductivity, good ductility, but its strength and durability are far less than that of steel.

3. Applications—Used for electrical wires, roofs, pipes, decorations, etc.

(B) Aluminum Category:

1. Overview—Extracted from alumina by removing oxygen.

2. General Properties—The lightest in specific gravity, only 0.82 pounds per cubic foot. Highly conductive and has great strength.

3. Applications—Household items, also used as an additive in copper.

(C) Lead, Zinc, Tin, Nickel, etc. Category:

1. Overview—All refined from ore.

2. Applications—All mixed into copper and iron to impart various properties and effects.

(3) Alloys:

(A) Brass:

1. Overview—An alloy of copper and zinc.

2. Properties—Resistant to corrosion.

3. Applications—Used for hinges.

(B) White Copper (Paktong):

1. Overview—An alloy of copper and tin.

2. Properties—Resistant to corrosion; more valuable than pure copper.

3. Applications—Used for hinges, decorations, etc.

Non-metallic building materials can be roughly divided into eight categories, listed as follows:

(A) Wood Category:

1. Overview—Cut from forests in the mountains.

2. General Properties—Easy for temporary construction, easy to cut down, and strong when subjected to small external forces.

3. Applications—Can be used for wallboards, pillars, beams, horizontal bars, and rafters.

(B) Cement and Aggregate Category:

1. Overview—Cement is made by roasting limestone, clay, etc. Aggregate is a mixture of cement, sand, water, and gravel, also known as reinforced concrete.

2. General Properties—Strong in compression but weak in tension.

3. Applications—Can be used for plastering walls, laying foundations, and pouring floors.

(C) Mortar:

1. Overview—Made by mixing cement, clean water, lime, and sand.

2. General Properties—Extremely adhesive.

3. Applications—Used for plastering walls and bonding bricks and stones.

(D) Brick Category:

1. Overview—Bricks include gray bricks and ceramic bricks, all made by firing clay.

2. General Properties—Hard and brittle, with high compressive strength.

3. Applications—Can be used for building walls and stacking partitions. (To be continued)

Letter to the Editor 232

To the esteemed Editor,

Having read the section concerning a certain specialized school on Jiangxi Road, as mentioned by you in the "Letters" column of issue 108, it is entirely inconsistent with the facts. The reason why our school added an advanced class in the Department of Architecture was in response to requests from various parties. It specializes in teaching reinforced concrete and steel construction design and calculation techniques. The intention is to cater to those who already have a foundation in drafting but lack the ability to calculate reinforced concrete. It is estimated that the course can be completed in six months. The course only covers two subjects, and students already have a foundation in drafting, so they can master the skills within this half year. We have never claimed it to be a "higher architecture discipline," and the name "advanced class" is only relative to the beginner-level class. Your assumption of the term "higher architecture discipline" is clearly inconsistent with the facts. Here is the advertisement that our school previously distributed, to clarify the facts: "Our school is now adding an advanced class in the Department of Architecture in response to various requests. We have hired the German architect Mr. Hoffbin to serve as professor and head of the Department of Architecture. The advanced class specializes in teaching reinforced concrete and steel construction design and calculation techniques. Classes are held every Tuesday and Thursday evening from 7 PM to 9 PM. The monthly tuition is thirty yuan, and the course lasts for six months. Anyone who has a foundation in drafting, can understand English lectures, and wishes to further their studies to register with the Ministry of Industry, please register quickly and pay a registration fee of two yuan to reserve a spot and avoid missing out."

The strict enforcement of the industrial technician registration regulations by the Ministry of Industry is indeed true. It is not easy for those who did not graduate from a school to be approved as technicians, and even applying to register as assistant technicians is difficult. It is also common for applicants to be summoned to Beijing for an interview. Therefore, those who did not graduate from a school and intend to register with the Ministry of Industry must have a thorough understanding of reinforced concrete calculation techniques to be confident. Our school established the advanced class to facilitate those who want to supplement their knowledge. The advertisement does not imply "registration upon completion of the course." How can you say it is "using registration as bait"?

The tuition fee is based on practical considerations. With six students, the monthly tuition revenue is one hundred and eighty yuan, which is not excessive. I do not know what you are basing your claim of "fraudulent behavior" on. Furthermore, the term "fraud" is a criminal offense under the law. If the other party does not engage in such behavior, the accuser will be subject to retaliation. Our school is in its early stages, and everything is being created from scratch. We are willing to sincerely accept guidance or criticism. If you believe the tuition fee is too high, there is room for discussion. Furthermore, our school added the advanced class to provide supplementary education for both Chinese and foreign students in the same class. It is not "flaunting foreigners to attract attention." The logic is clear. If you hope to provide benevolent guidance, our school is still willing to sincerely accept it. Your publication's principles are upright and respected. We hope your intention is not malicious. Since you have published the original letter, we hope you will also grant publication to this letter. We are grateful for your assistance. Best regards. Zhizhi Hai Vocational School, February 15th.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

Rambling Talk by the Big-Mouthed Comedian Joe E. Brown 233

— Xi Lin

Joe E. Brown's greatest talent is making people laugh, but he also has his serious moments. When a Hollywood film magazine invited him to be an honorary editor for a day, sitting at the editor's desk, he wrote the following serious article. It can be considered an editorial, and although the words are rambling, they still have some sense. Therefore, I have translated it:

The first point he discusses is "The Obligation of Stars." He says: "Movie stars often talk about their artistic obligations to fans—how to maintain a certain standard in their work. That's great! But in my opinion, there's something equally important: they must remember that they also have a moral responsibility to the public who admire them. That means their behavior and personal affairs should have an uplifting effect on the public.

"On this point, I'm not saying that movie stars have to wear a moralistic face all day long, never joking or laughing. I'm not saying they have to get up early every day to sing hymns and pray before meals. But I believe they must be very careful about their personal morality and their actions in public places, and be an example to society. Simply put, I believe a movie star has the power to encourage people to improve, but also to influence them to become degenerate. I have children myself, so perhaps I take this issue too seriously, but I feel that all movie stars, occupying an important position in the public's mind, should have this awareness."

The second point Joe E. Brown mentions is "Stars Can't Deceive." He says: "When ordinary people hear about how romantic life is in Hollywood, they should remember: stars can't deceive the camera. Lust and insomnia will always show on their faces, and there's no hiding it. Filming starts at nine o'clock. They have to get up at six-thirty in the morning. If they can leave the set at six in the afternoon, they're lucky. After leaving the set, removing makeup and changing clothes takes at least another hour. So they don't get home for dinner until seven in the evening at the earliest. After dinner, there are many things to prepare for the next day's work. If they also need seven or eight hours of sleep, they simply don't have any time to be reckless. In short, Hollywood is not a place for reckless people to stay for long. If they want to stay in Hollywood, they can't be reckless. Please don't believe the rumors!"

The third point is "Hollywood Children." He says: "Hollywood children are very happy. This isn't because their parents earn a lot of money, giving them the finest food, housing, and education. It's really because the people in the film industry raise their children in a very good and commendable way. The people gathered in Hollywood now are very noble men and women, and their descendants will certainly not let their parents down when they grow up. But there's one thing I hope: that Hollywood won't become too big, so that there's no space for children to play. Children can't always play in the garden; they need a large space to dig caves and play cowboys. Open space is essential for any society. The open space in Hollywood is gradually becoming insufficient."

The fourth point he makes is "Hollywood Has Changed." He says: "Hollywood has changed, and you can see it from the Christmas gifts. In the past, every Christmas in Hollywood, everyone would give each other gifts of diamonds or platinum. Stars would give directors new sports cars and square-cut gemstones. Set designers and lighting technicians knew they were out of favor if they didn't receive three or four watches by Christmas. Female reporters usually received at least a set of silverware. Everyone used the most expensive gifts to express their affection.

"But this year it's different! Almost everyone is using their brains to buy reasonable things, and buying very little. If they have extra money, they're buying everyday items to distribute to the poor. Hollywood has really made a lot of progress in this regard, and the knowledge and insights are all lessons learned from the recession."

Joe E. Brown visited Shanghai last year. His impressions of China are also mentioned in his essay. He says: "When I arrived in China, I didn't feel like a movie star was anything special. But I enjoyed more freedom because the Chinese people didn't chase after stars for autographs, although they liked to meet and talk with stars. I like the Chinese people very much because I believe their friendly attitude is very sincere."

Soviet Film Exhibition Delegates Zhou Jianyun and Hu Die to Depart Soon 234

The international film exhibition initiated by the Soviet Union previously solicited entries from our country and telegraphed invitations to Mr. Zhou Jianyun, manager of the Star Film Company, Ms. Hu Die, a famous actress, and representatives from the Lianhua Film Company to attend and participate. After the central government repeatedly summoned Mr. Zhou to Beijing to discuss, and selected "Empty Valley Orchid," "Sisters Flowers," "The Torrents," "Spring Silkworms," "Song of the Fishermen," "The Highway," "Bigamy," and "Woman" as entries, the first batch of delegates, including Mr. Tao Bosun from Lianhua Film Company, departed a week ago. The second batch of delegates, Mr. Zhou Jianyun and Ms. Hu Die, will also depart around the 20th, boarding a special ship with Ambassador Yan Huiqing and Mei Wan Hua. Mr. Zhou's wife, Ms. Chen Yujun, studied political economy at Waseda University in Japan and plans to accompany him to undertake research and recording work. The Star Film Company is actively preparing a large number of photos and printed materials (all with Russian translations) to bring with them.

Mr. Zhou's responsibilities at the Star Film Company are extremely heavy. This time, he is taking time out to go abroad and is busy preparing. Mr. Zhou's friends, such as Pan Gongzhan, Tang Youren, Ouyang Yuqian, Chen Biling, Chen Yanbin, Pan Yousheng, Gao Zhanfei, the Soviet consul and his wife, various film trading companies, Nanyang film merchants, local and foreign theater managers, the press, the literary and art circles, and colleagues from the Star Film Company, a total of more than thirty groups, have been hosting banquets to bid farewell to Mr. and Mrs. Zhou and Ms. Hu Die, making him extremely busy.

This overseas expedition of our country's film industry is an unprecedented move, and its significance is very important. According to Mr. Zhou's statement, he has heavy responsibilities in the film industry and is deeply interested in film culture. Therefore, he is very willing to take the opportunity to participate in the international film exhibition to see the cultural construction of the new Soviet Union. He believes that he can learn a lot from others, and the spirit of the Russians' hard work is also worthy of our emulation.

Taking the opportunity to attend the Soviet International Film Exhibition, Mr. Zhou also plans to conduct a detailed inspection of the film industry. He has drafted the following outline for the inspection: (1) The Soviet Union's current film administrative management agency, organizational system, film censorship tax rules, import procedures, etc., (2) The current situation of the film industry, (3) Film schools, (4) Construction and equipment of film studios, (5) Movie theaters, (6) Music and drama, (7) Books and magazines related to film, (8) Whether there is a market for Chinese films, (9) The Soviet Union's impressions and criticisms of Chinese entries, (10) Overseas Chinese opinions on domestic films, (11) The proceedings of the Soviet International Film Exhibition, (12) Other.

It is also heard that if time permits, Mr. Zhou and others also intend to travel to Germany, France, and Italy to see the industries of Berlin and the ancient sites of Rome.

— Lin Qin

(1)

In 1935, film songs were very popular. Sound was inserted, and silent films were dubbed. Almost every film had "songs," and every film was "dubbed"!

Playwrights may have a way out, because some directors have abandoned "writing and directing themselves"!

Guarantees to Amaze You 236

— Qi Guan

The advertisement for RKO Pictures, the three letters R.K.O., are 67 feet high on top of Pifreri Mountain in Hollywood, and each letter is 40 feet wide. The electricity bill costs hundreds of dollars per month. There are iron ladders on each letter. Someone previously climbed up the iron ladder and jumped to commit suicide. Now, people are assigned to guard them day and night.

MGM has 2,000 pieces of transportation equipment, including light trains, automobiles, carriages, oxcarts, sedan chairs, airplanes, and 50 specially made armored large cars.

Universal Pictures covers more than 600 acres, with mountains, rivers, and wilderness. There are shops inside, and a huge hospital, where people in the film industry often stay for treatment.

In Europe, Ufa Film Company in Germany is the largest, with more than 1,000 acres of land. There are small electric trains to pick up and drop off people from the gate to the internal offices. If you walk around the Ufa Company, it would take 20 hours to complete the entire film studio!

Fox Movietone City is like a small city, divided into ten areas. The distribution of electricity uses 70 miles of underground tunnels to connect the power lines, which is almost as complex as the electrical distribution in New York City.

Warner Brothers-First National's film studio has 50 huge buildings, covering 90 acres. The offices cover 50 acres, and there is also a huge square, with mountains and rivers, covering more than 800 acres. After First National Pictures merged into Warner Brothers in 1928, more than 200 acres of huge buildings were added.

There are more than 700 mountains in California, USA, and half of them are occupied by Hollywood film companies, preparing for filming.

Seventeen islands around San Francisco all have offices of various Hollywood film companies, and are registered as film-specific land.

If Hollywood's film industry were to stop, the market in the entire state of California would probably decline as a result.

A Bundle of Tianyi Tidbits 237

— Bai Yun

The script work for "Three Women in a Storm" has been completed, but the selection of the three leading actresses in the film will be carefully considered.

Wang Bin's recent second script, titled "Sleepless City," is said to have been completely drafted. The entire play is set at night.

Gao Tianqi returned to Shaoxing to play during the Spring Festival, so his novel "Cotton Padded Jacket" has not yet been released.

Shao Weihe, a recording technician at Tianyi, recently returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong.

Liangyou Company will publish "The Spectacle of Chinese Stars" and is soliciting photos of major stars. Yesterday, photographer Zhou Shilu took many photos for Fan Xuepeng, Lu Lixia, and others.

Chen Yumei's records are selling well, among which the famous ones such as "Lullaby", "Lotus Picking Song", "Taiping Flower", "Flower Selling Song" have endless increase.

Kuaihuolin Recruits Actors 238

Kuaihuolin Film Company is recruiting 30 male and female actors. As long as you love movies, can speak Mandarin, and have a junior high school education, you can go to apply. Please go to the management office of Kuaihuolin Film Company, No. 1 Renchang Lane, at the intersection of Kaizi Road and Songshan Road, Shanghai, from 1 PM to 4 PM every day. Please bring a recent 4-inch photo.

Film Novel

National Voice (Bordertown) (4) 239

— Xuemei

After Johnny Ramirez finished speaking, the leader of the five men spoke: "Charlie, did you say these words, or did this guy say them? Why can't you speak for yourself, and you have to let someone else speak for you? Are you kidding us in front of us? We bought that piece of land, and you'll regret it." Before Charlie could speak, Johnny interjected, "Of course you're not kidding. We also hope you don't joke. Because if you want to buy that piece of land, you'll have to buy it from us." The man said, "I don't understand what you're saying." Johnny said, "What I'm saying is that we have the right of first refusal to buy that land. You need to know that we knew your trick months ago and have been prepared."

After Johnny finished speaking, he walked out, still smiling. The men sat there without saying a word. Finally, one person said, "Where did you hire this person from?" Charlie Roque had already recovered and said with a smile, "Really smart, isn't he? Friends, let me tell you, this is my secret: to be able to use people, to have smart people come to me. He came to me six months ago, originally extremely bored, looking for work. He met Bu Qu'ande Luosi, my boxer, a wild bull with immense strength. Bu Qu'ande Luosi asked him, 'Fool, what can you do?' Johnny said calmly, 'Idiot, what can you do, what can I do?' Bu Qu'ande Luosi heard this and roared like a lion, rushing towards Johnny. That's all Bu Qu'ande Luosi could remember, I'm afraid... By the time he woke up leisurely an hour later, his nose was bent, and his position was gone."

The man said, "Did you chase Bu Qu'ande Luosi away?" Charlie said, "Of course, what I like most is the victor." He paused and said, "What are we doing sitting here? Why don't you go outside for a drink?" So they went outside, under the colorful lights, the gambling tables were noisy, and the sound of money clanking. Charlie Roque couldn't help but be happy. At this time, Roque's wife, Mary Roque, was walking in from outside. His wife, Mary Roque, was the most fashionable woman in Mexicali. Her hair was golden. Her figure was sensual, with curves. She also had a pair of arrogant and seductive eyes.

Roque saw her come in and hurried to greet her, saying, "Honey, why did you come here?" Mary replied listlessly, "Do you find it strange?" Her beautiful eyes glanced at Johnny Ramirez. Roque said, "It's not strange, but my little sister, I don't like you coming to this kind of place. You know, this is not a place for women." His little sister said, "I can't stay at home all day and all night. I also want to go out and have some fun. What can I do at home? Feed the goldfish? But the goldfish only eat once a day..." Roque said with a smile, "Be good, don't make a fuss, go home quickly... I'll be back earlier today." He turned his head and shouted to Johnny, "Johnny, take the wife home."

So Johnny accompanied the boss's wife out, walking between many wine tables. They walked out the door. Johnny opened the door for her without saying a word. They walked to the street. Mary hooked her arms around Johnny's neck and kissed him. A very quick and passionate kiss. After she kissed him, she jumped into the car and drove away laughing. Johnny stood dumbly on the side of the road. He couldn't help but feel something, but he had to be careful. He didn't have to get involved with Mary Roque because he had more important things to do tonight. (To be continued)
